links[i].getAttribute('href');\n\n                //console.log(url_atual)\n\n                if(url_atual != null){\n\n                    if( url_atual.startsWith(\"/\") ){\n\n }\n\n        //função que remove as datas dos modais\n        function removeDataInicial(links){\n\n            for (let i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {\n\n                //removendo a data-inicial dos modais internos\n                if(links[i].hasAttribute(\"data-inicial\")){\n\n                    links[i].removeAttribute(\"data-inicial\");\n                }\n\n                let url_atual
